        function updaterightpannel(id) {
            if (id == 1) {
                document.getElementById("CricketSchedule").style.display = "";
                document.getElementById("CricketResults").style.display = "none";


                document.getElementById("RightPan1").className = "ActivTabRight";
                document.getElementById("RightPan2").className = "InActivTabRight";

            } else {
                document.getElementById("CricketSchedule").style.display = "none";
                document.getElementById("CricketResults").style.display = "";


                document.getElementById("RightPan1").className = "InActivTabRight";
                document.getElementById("RightPan2").className = "ActivTabRight";
            }
        }

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
        function callAHAH(url, pageElement, callMessage, errorMessage) {
            document.getElementById(pageElement).innerHTML = callMessage;
            try {
                req = new XMLHttpRequest(); /* e.g. Firefox */
            } catch (e) {
                try {
                    req = new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");  /* some versions IE */
                } catch (e) {
                    try {
                        req = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");  /* some versions IE */
                    } catch (E) {
                        req = false;
                    }
                }
            }
            req.onreadystatechange = function () { responseAHAH(pageElement, errorMessage); };
            req.open("GET", url, true);
            req.send(null);
        }

        function responseAHAH(pageElement, errorMessage) {
            var output = '';
            if (req.readyState == 4) {
                if (req.status == 200) {
                    output = req.responseText;
                    document.getElementById(pageElement).innerHTML = output;
                } else {
                    document.getElementById(pageElement).innerHTML = errorMessage + "\n" + output;
                }
            }
        }
        setInterval(function () { doSomething(); }, 60000);
        function doSomething() {
            var d = new Date();
            if (/Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
//callAHAH('HomeTxt/Live.txt?' + d.getTime(), 'contentH', 'Loading Wait...', 'Error');
            }
            else
            {
callAHAH('HomeTxt/Live.txt?' + d.getTime(), 'contentRB', 'Loading Wait...', 'Error');
            }
        }
        function resizeIframe() {
          
          document.getElementById("CS").style.height = document.getElementById("CS").contentWindow.document.body.scrollHeight + "px";
      }
</script>

<section class="cat-box column2 tie-cat-6 ">
<div class="cat-box-title">
&nbsp; <small class="textPurp" style="TEXT-TRANSFORM:uppercase;FONT-SIZE:20px"><a href="/recipes/">
Food &amp; Recipes</a> </small>
</div>
<div class="cat-box-content" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: green 0px solid; BORDER-TOP: #017A47 1px solid">
<font style="FONT-SIZE:2px">
<br>
<br>
</font>
<table class="TextClass" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="3" width="100%">
<tbody><tr>
<td valign="top" align="center" width="160"><img width="150" src="http://hamariweb.com/recipes/images/recipeicon/9316.jpg" class="image"><br>
Recipe of The Day</td>
<td valign="top">
